          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              BEAM Teknoloji is an Accredited Cyber Security Testing and Evaluation Laboratory established in 2011. Founded with the mission to safeguard organizations against the complex landscape of digital threats, BEAM has been providing cutting-edge cybersecurity solutions and services working with multiple clients across various sectors and regions and has played a crucial role in bolstering the cyber resilience of critical infrastructures. 

Our Differentiation
- Domain experience: We conducted over one thousand formal product evaluations across various industries including government, defense contractors, telecommunications, financial services, transportation, healthcare, and energy.
- Holistic Security Framework: Our Managed Security Services are structured around a comprehensive framework, designed to guide our customers through the complexities of cybersecurity governance, threat prevention, user access security, and data privacy.
- Experienced Team: With a dedicated in-house team of security experts and trusted advisors, we bring a wealth of knowledge and experience to all our clients.
 - Vendor-Agnostic Approach: We provide unbiased advice and solutions, selecting the most suitable technologies and services for building an agile and robust security strategy. 

Our services include;
- Security Assessment of Critical Infrastructures including SCADA, IoT Systems, Databases and Applications, Network Components 
- Common Criteria Assessment and Formal Product Certification
- Penetration Testing and Vulnerability Assessment
- SOC Managed Services

Our achievements;
- 1000+ Products Tested and Certified
- 1M+ Users of Phishing Platform
- 10M+ Lines of Codes Evaluated

At BeamSec, we see a clear takeaway: digital nativity must be matched with digital defense. Security programs need to meet Gen Z where they are â€” interactive, engaging, and built for the platforms they live on.

Because being â€œborn digitalâ€ should never mean being â€œborn vulnerable.â€

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Your strongest firewall isnâ€™t code. Itâ€™s people.

90% of cyber breaches start with human error:
- clicking a fake link
- downloading a â€œtoo good to be trueâ€ file
- reusing weak passwords

That means culture is as important as code.
Training teams to think like hackers, question every link, and spot red flags can reduce breaches more than any shiny new tool.

ğŸ‘‰ Cybersecurity starts with awareness. Defense starts with you.</p>
